        {"@context":"http://schema.org","@type":"SoftwareApplication","name":"The Greedy Cave","description":"In a land far, far away there once was a vast continent called Milton. It was a land where the power of rule came by the sword and the arcane, where Men who devoted themselves to the blade or to magecraft, could become the finest warriors, wisest wizards or the greatest adventurers. In this land, there are several kingdoms divided by borders but united through history. Countless stories of alliances, upheaval, and moments of peace bedeck this tapestry, but that is a tale for another day. \n\nOur story begins in a remote kingdom to the north, Iblis, an obscure and oft-forgotten place. It is a wild and barren land, a place where its people scrape a living from the earth, mining minerals for the lords of the south. On occasion, adventurers would stop by for the night but never linger. Until one day, a fledgling adventurer lost his way and stumbled into a hole. The story might have ended then had he not come back, but return he did, with sacks of gold and glittering treasure. \n\nLike a fierce gale from the north, news of his fame and fortune fanned across the kingdoms overnight, and kings sent their bravest warriors and adventurers to clear the cavern of monsters in search of treasure. Even peasants wanting a part of this newfound wealth partook in these expeditions. In no time at all, a bustling town had sprung up in this forgotten place. People set up camps, and formed their own groups to explore the cave. Clever merchants not missing this opportunity, built taverns and shops near the cave, selling equipment and potions to eager adventurers. At first, everything seemed fine. As explorers delved into the caves, they encountered new creatures and discovered new treasures. Mysteries continued to pour forth from the cave, yet nobody knew where the source of the secrets lay. However, as the explorations continued, the balance of wealth beyond the cave began to waver, and cracks appeared among those adventurers who had previously worked arm-in-arm. The latecomers or weak, limited to wandering the upper levels of the cave, could only watch as the veteran adventurers brought treasure after treasure from the deep. They began harboring dark thoughts as they watched the veteran adventurers grow arrogant from their largesse, ordering people around, hoarding secrets from the rest. The place became a festering pool of suspicions and greed, mired in a jealous rage. \n\nIt started with an adventurer disappearing in the cave. Rumors circulated he had found some legendary treasure and hoarded it for himself. Others said he had been guided to another world by some mysterious magic force in the cave. Still, the unspoken belief was that he had been murdered by a rival party and was buried somewhere beneath the caverns. Nobody knows exactly what happened, but people have continued to disappear ever since. As more people have gone missing, some adventurers have called it quits, others cling to hope, and a few continue to wait and see. Which brings us to you, an ordinary young man, coming into this extraordinary circumstance with purposes unknown to others.   <section class="l-content-width section section--bordered">
    <div class="section__description">
      <h2 class="section__headline visuallyhidden">Miêu tả</h2>
      <div class="l-row">
          <div class="we-truncate we-truncate--multi-line we-truncate--interactive  we-truncate--truncated l-column small-12 medium-9 large-8" dir="">
      

        <div data-clamp="" class="we-clamp" ismorertl="false" style="height: 90px; mask: linear-gradient(0deg, rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px, rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 18px, rgb(0, 0, 0) 18px), linear-gradient(270deg, rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px, rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 32.8px, rgb(0, 0, 0) 68.8px);">
  <p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">In a land far, far away there once was a
 vast continent called Milton. It was a land where the power of rule 
came by the sword and the arcane, where Men who devoted themselves to 
the blade or to magecraft, could become the finest warriors, wisest 
wizards or the greatest adventurers. In this land, there are several 
kingdoms divided by borders but united through history. Countless 
stories of alliances, upheaval, and moments of peace bedeck this 
tapestry, but that is a tale for another day.</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">Our story begins in a remote kingdom to 
the north, Iblis, an obscure and oft-forgotten place. It is a wild and 
barren land, a place where its people scrape a living from the earth, 
mining minerals for the lords of the south. On occasion, adventurers 
would stop by for the night but never linger. Until one day, a fledgling
 adventurer lost his way and stumbled into a hole. The story might have 
ended then had he not come back, but return he did, with sacks of gold 
and glittering treasure.</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">Like a fierce gale from the north, news 
of his fame and fortune fanned across the kingdoms overnight, and kings 
sent their bravest warriors and adventurers to clear the cavern of 
monsters in search of treasure. Even peasants wanting a part of this 
newfound wealth partook in these expeditions. In no time at all, a 
bustling town had sprung up in this forgotten place. People set up 
camps, and formed their own groups to explore the cave. Clever merchants
 not missing this opportunity, built taverns and shops near the cave, 
selling equipment and potions to eager adventurers. At first, everything
 seemed fine. As explorers delved into the caves, they encountered new 
creatures and discovered new treasures. Mysteries continued to pour 
forth from the cave, yet nobody knew where the source of the secrets 
lay. However, as the explorations continued, the balance of wealth 
beyond the cave began to waver, and cracks appeared among those 
adventurers who had previously worked arm-in-arm. The latecomers or 
weak, limited to wandering the upper levels of the cave, could only 
watch as the veteran adventurers brought treasure after treasure from 
the deep. They began harboring dark thoughts as they watched the veteran
 adventurers grow arrogant from their largesse, ordering people around, 
hoarding secrets from the rest. The place became a festering pool of 
suspicions and greed, mired in a jealous rage.</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">It started with an adventurer 
disappearing in the cave. Rumors circulated he had found some legendary 
treasure and hoarded it for himself. Others said he had been guided to 
another world by some mysterious magic force in the cave. Still, the 
unspoken belief was that he had been murdered by a rival party and was 
buried somewhere beneath the caverns. Nobody knows exactly what 
happened, but people have continued to disappear ever since. As more 
people have gone missing, some adventurers have called it quits, others 
cling to hope, and a few continue to wait and see. Which brings us to 
you, an ordinary young man, coming into this extraordinary circumstance 
with purposes unknown to others. May you find what you seek in ...</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">--------------------------------------------------------</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">In " The Greedy Cave", you are a brave adventurer tasked with exploring a mysterious cave and battling all kinds of monsters.</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">Use your wits to defeat them, learn 
different skills, gain mighty equipment, challenge evil monster bosses, 
and decipher the mystery surrounding this cave...</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">Game Features</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">·Randomly generated cave levels provide a different game experience every time!</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">·Hundreds of monsters to defeat!</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">·Hundreds of equipment to collect!</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">·Hundreds of quests and achievements to conquer!</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">·Enchant/Reform/Level up/Gold collecting, and more abundant systems to explore!</p>
<br>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">Contact us</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">cs.thegreedycave@avalongames.com</p>
<p dir="ltr" data-test-bidi="">https://www.facebook.com/greedycave/</p>
</div>

        thêm
